```text
17.14. Regarding The Quintessential Quintuplets 
17.14.1. The order zone may also be regarded as 
“memory” by some card effects. 
17.14.1.1. The regarding of the order zone as 
“memory” has no meaning in terms of rules, 
but can be referenced by other effects. 
 
17.15. Regarding CoroCoro Collab Pack 
17.15.1. The “Dangerous Skill” keyword is a keyword 
that some abilities have. 
17.15.1.1. The “Dangerous Skill” keyword has no 
meaning in terms of rules, but can be 
referenced by other effects. 
17.15.1.2. “Dangerous Skill” may be indicated on 
cards with the  icon. 
17.15.2. The “Retry” keyword ability is a continuous 
ability that means “This card can retry”. 
17.15.2.1. “Retry” may be indicated on cards with 
the  icon. 
17.15.2.2. To “Retry a unit” means “If that unit has 
the Retry ability, stand that unit, and until end 
of turn, that unit cannot Retry, and that unit 
gets Power +5000 and “[AUTO](VC/RC):At the 
beginning of your next stand step, until end of 
turn, this unit’s critical and drive increase or 
decrease to one, and lose this ability.”. 
17.15.3. “Version Up” is an activation condition 
keyword (14.2) that references whether units or 
damage have fulfilled specific conditions. 
17.15.3.1. Version Up is written as “(ability type 
icon)-Version Up:(ability)”. 
17.15.3.2. Version Up’s activation condition is 
fulfilled by either the unit with this keyword 
having persona rode (7.15.1.4) this turn, or by 
this unit’s master’s damage zone having 4 or 
more cards, or by having both. 
17.15.3.3. “Version Up” may be indicated on cards 
with the  icon. 
17.15.4. “Deal” is a keyword that a series of abilities 
that put units in the deal state have. 
17.15.4.1. The deal state has no meaning in terms 
of rules, but can be referenced by other 
effects. 
17.15.4.2. “Deal” may be indicated on cards with 
the  icon. 
17.15.5. The “Oversized” keyword is a keyword that 
a series of abilities that put units in the oversized 
state have. 
17.15.5.1. “Oversized” may be indicated on cards 
with the  icon. 
17.15.6. The “Explosive Growth” keyword ability is a 
continuous ability that allows a special method of 
calling. 
17.15.6.1. Explosive Growth is written as 
“Explosive Growth-(unit condition)”. 
17.15.6.2. When normal calling a unit with 
Explosive Growth, if the circle that unit is being 
called to has a unit that fulfills (unit condition), 
instead of retiring the unit that was on that 
circle (6.2.3.4), that unit’s main type becomes 
“growth factor”, becomes associated with the 
unit with Explosive Growth that is being normal 
called as its growth factor, and put that unit 
being normal called in the explosive growth 
state. 
17.15.6.2.1. Effects that are applied to the card 
that became a growth factor remain while it is 
a growth factor, but are not applied while it is 
not a unit.
```

### Page 50

```text
17.15.6.3. As long as a unit in the explosive growth 
state has a growth factor associated with it, it is 
considered to be in the Explosive Growth state. 
17.15.6.4. When a unit in the explosive growth 
state moves to another zone, as long as that is 
not a “leave its growth factor and return to 
(specified zone)” process, the growth factor 
card associated with that unit moves to that 
zone at the same time. 
17.15.6.5. “Explosive Growth” may be indicated on 
cards with the  icon. 
17.15.6.6. When there is an instruction to 
“Explosive Growth” a card with the Explosive 
Growth ability to a unit on the field, call that 
card with the Explosive Growth ability to the 
circle that unit is on. 
17.15.6.7. “Leave this unit’s growth factor on this 
rear-guard circle and return (specified unit) to 
(specified zone)” is a special action that means 
“move (specified unit) to (specified zone), the 
main type of the growth factor associated with 
it becomes unit, and cancel that association”. 
 
17.16. Regarding Buddyfight 
17.16.1. Cards with “Buddyfight” indicated for their 
nation are Buddyfight-related cards. 
17.16.2. Each Buddyfight-related card has an icon for 
the World they belong to. 
 
Dragon World 
 
Danger World 
 
Magic World 
 
Katana World 
 
Ancient World 
 
Legend World 
 
Darkness Dragon 
World 
 
Hero World 
 
Dragon Ein 
 
Parade of Hundred 
Demons 
 
Generic 
 
17.16.2.1. Worlds may be referenced as “<(World 
name)>” in text. 
17.16.3. “Flag” is a continuous ability that changes 
the number of cards that can be included in a 
deck. 
17.16.3.1. Only one card with the “Flag” ability can 
be included in a deck. 
17.16.4. Players may become “Buddyfighters” from 
effects. When a player becomes a Buddyfighter, 
perform the following. 
17.16.4.1. That player chooses a unit card from 
their ride deck, and puts it into the order zone. 
17.16.4.1.1. Cards with the card name of the card 
put in the order zone from this are regarded 
as the “Buddy Monster” for that player for the 
duration of this game. 
17.16.4.2. A player being a Buddyfighter has no 
particular meaning in terms of rules. 
17.16.5. As a result of cards put in the crest zone, 
players may have “gauge”. 
17.16.5.1. Cards in the crest zone that allow 
players to have “gauge” are called “gauge 
crests”. 
17.16.5.2. When a Buddyfight-related card simply 
refers to “gauge”, it refers to cards in the gauge 
zone associated with the gauge crest that 
player is the master of. 
17.16.5.3. When a player gains a card as “gauge” 
from a Buddyfight-related card, move that card 
to the gauge zone, and associate it with the 
gauge crest that player is the master of. 
17.16.5.4. When there is an instruction from a 
Buddyfight-related card for a player to “pay 
(number) gauge”, that player moves (number)
```

### Page 51

```text
cards associated with the gauge crest that 
players is the master of to their drop zone. 
17.16.6. Players have a “Call Cost Zone” zone. 
17.16.6.1. The call cost zone is a public zone, and 
the order of cards in the call cost zone is not 
controlled. 
17.16.6.2. If a card enters the call cost zone from 
zone A, and then is put into zone B, that card is 
considered to have been put into zone B from 
zone A. 
17.16.7. Buddyfight-related rear-guards may have 1 
or more cards stacked under them. 
17.16.7.1. If there are multiple cards stacked on a 
rear-guard circle, the top card of that stack is 
regarded as the unit on that circle, and the rest 
of the cards are regarded as the “Buddy Soul” 
of the unit on that circle. 
17.16.7.2. Buddy Soul are not regarded as units on 
that circle. 
17.16.7.3. When a unit with Buddy Soul moves to 
another rear-guard circle, its Buddy Soul 
simultaneously moves to that destination. 
17.16.7.4. When a unit with Buddy Soul moves to a 
destination that is not a rear-guard circle or 
guardian circle, or moves from the guardian 
circle to another zone, all of its Buddy Soul is 
put into their master’s drop zone. 
17.16.7.5. When a unit with Buddy Soul is locked, 
that unit’s Buddy Soul becomes locked Buddy 
Soul on that lock circle that is associated with 
that locked card. Similarly, when a locked card 
is no longer in the locked state, if that locked 
card has locked Buddy Soul associated with it, 
they become that unit’s Buddy Soul at the 
same time as that card becomes no longer in 
the locked state. 
17.16.8. Some cards have a “Call Cost” that must be 
performed to call that card to a rear-guard circle. 
17.16.8.1. Call cost is indicated on cards as 
“ :(cost contents)”. 
17.16.8.2. If the unit to be called has a call cost, 
confirm whether the following processes can 
be performed with regards to the contents of 
the call cost. 
17.16.8.2.1. Move that unit being called to the call 
cost zone. 
17.16.8.2.2. If there is an instruction to “put 
(specified cards) into Buddy Soul” in the call 
cost, move those cards to the call cost zone. 
17.16.8.2.3. If there is an instruction to retire 
specific units, perform that. 
17.16.8.2.4. If there is an instruction to “put (card 
being called) on top” of a specific unit, 
specify a unit you are the master of that 
fulfills that condition. 
17.16.8.2.5. If there is an instruction to pay 
gauge, follow that instruction (17.16.5.4). 
17.16.8.3. If any of the contents of the call cost of 
the unit to be called cannot be performed 
during the processing of the call cost, that unit 
is not called, and is put into the drop zone. 
17.16.8.4. Perform the processes instructed by the 
call cost (17.16.8.2). 
17.16.8.4.1. If this unit with a call cost is being 
called from the deck due to an effect, after 
moving that unit from the deck to the call cost 
zone, perform the rest of that effect to its 
end, then perform the remaining processes 
of the call cost. 
17.16.8.5. Perform the calling of that unit. 
17.16.8.5.1. If there is an instruction to “put (card 
being called) on top” of a specific unit, put 
the card in the call cost zone into the circle 
that unit is on, then put the unit that was on 
that circle and that unit’s Buddy Soul into the 
Buddy Soul of the unit that was newly called. 
17.16.8.5.2. If there is no instruction to “put on 
top” in the call cost, put the card being called 
from the call cost zone to the called circle. 
17.16.8.5.3. If there is an instruction to “put 
(specified cards) into Buddy Soul”, stack the 
cards put into the call cost zone when 
processing that instruction (17.16.8.2.2) 
underneath the unit being called as that 
unit’s Buddy Soul at the same time as that 
unit is put in the called circle. 
17.16.8.6. If there is an instruction to “call (a unit) 
without paying its call cost”, that unit is called 
as if its call cost does not exist. 
17.16.9. The “Soulguard” keyword ability is a 
continuous ability with a replacement effect that 
prevents units from moving to other zones. 
17.16.9.1. “Soulguard” means “when this unit 
would move to a zone that is not a rear-guard 
circle or guardian circle from an effect or the 
result of a battle, other than for a cost, you may 
discard one of this unit’s Buddy Soul. If you do, 
instead of moving that unit to that zone, that 
unit does not move.”. 
17.16.9.2. “Soulguard” may be indicated on cards 
by the  icon. 
17.16.10. The “Arms” keyword ability that Buddyfight-
related cards have is a continuous ability that 
some order cards have. 
17.16.10.1. The arms ability is indicated on cards 
as “Arms – (arms condition)”. 
17.16.10.2. Order cards with the arms ability are 
arms orders (17.7), and follow the rules 
regarding arms orders with the following 
exceptions. 
17.16.10.3. Cards with the arms ability can only be 
played if the player is a Buddyfighter (17.16.4). 
17.16.10.4. Cards with the arms ability can only be 
armed to units that fulfill the arms condition. 
17.16.10.5. If multiple cards with the arms ability 
are armed, only the newest remains while the 
others are put into the drop zone as a rule 
action. 
17.16.10.6. When vanguard that’s armed with a 
card with the arms ability is rode upon, that 
card becomes armed to the vanguard that was 
ridden. 
17.16.11. Cards may become “in the Link Attack 
state” from the effect of Buddyfight-related cards. 
17.16.11.1. While there is a unit in the Link Attack 
state, the power of the attacking unit of a battle
```

### Page 52

```text
is increased by a value equal to the power of 
that unit in the Link Attack state. 
17.16.11.1.1. If there is a change in the power of 
a unit in the Link Attack state during a battle, 
the power of the attacking also changes 
accordingly (11.11.1.8). 
17.16.11.2. A unit in the Link Attack state is no 
longer in the Link Attack state at the point 
when the current battle ends. 
17.16.12. Specific information may become ∞ from 
the effect of Buddyfight-related cards. 
17.16.12.1. If there is an instruction for specific 
information to “become ∞”, that numerical 
value becomes 0, and that information 
becomes the ∞ state. 
17.16.12.1.1. If there is an instruction for 
information to become the same value as 
information that is in the ∞ state, that 
information becomes the ∞ state. 
17.16.12.2. When a numerical value is added to or 
subtracted from information in the ∞ state, it 
is added to or subtracted from that 
information’s numerical value. 
17.16.12.3. If there is an instruction for information 
in the ∞ state to become a specified value 
that is not ∞, that information is no longer in 
the ∞ state, and becomes that specified 
value. 
17.16.12.4. When information in the ∞ state is 
compared to numerical values or information 
that is not in the ∞ state, the information in 
the ∞ state is always regarded to be larger. If 
information in the ∞ state are compared with 
each other, their numerical values are 
compared. 
17.16.13. Some order cards have an ability to be 
called to the guardian circle as trigger units 
during your guard step. Unless there is a specific 
zone instructed, such cards can only be called 
from the player’s hand. 
17.16.14. Buddyfight-related cards may have abilities 
with the following keywords. These keywords 
have no meaning in terms of the rules, but may 
be referenced by other abilities and effects. 
 Buddy Call 
 My Buddy! 
 Jackknife Braveheart 
 Great Spell, Saturday Night Devil 
Fever 
 Clear Serenity 
 [Double Attack] (indicated by the 
 icon) 
 Dragon Throne 
 “Thunder Mine” 
 Hundred Demons Sorcery, Evil Pulse 
 Shadow Dive 
 
Section 18. Miscellaneous 
 
18.1. Loop 
18.1.1. When some effects are applied, sometimes 
you can do a set of actions any number of times, 
or you must repeat a set of actions an infinite 
number of times. This is called a loop, and the 
cycle of actions is called a “loop action set“. If it 
happens, then proceed in the following manner: 
18.1.1.1. If nobody can stop the loop, then the 
game ends in draw. 
18.1.1.2. If only one player can choose to stop the 
loop, then he or she chooses the number of 
times that loop repeats, assumes that the loop 
action set was performed that number of times, 
then chooses to stop at any action that can 
stop the loop. Then, if all game situations are 
the same as when the loop had occurred, then 
players cannot choose to do the loop again 
except if it were to be forced by automatic 
abilities. 
18.1.1.3. If both players can choose to stop the 
loop, then the turn player chooses the number 
of times that loop repeats, then the non-turn 
player chooses the number of times to repeat. 
The smaller number is chosen as the number 
of times to repeat the loop action set, and the 
player who chose the smaller number chooses 
to stop at any action that can stop the loop. 
Then, if all game situations are the same as 
when the loop had occurred) all cards in all 
zones are the same), then the player who 
chose the bigger number cannot choose to do 
the loop again except if it were to be forced by 
automatic abilities. 
18.1.1.4. The actions in a loop action set are not 
resolved individually, but are all resolved at the 
same time, omitting the intermediate actions. 
However, even though the actions are omitted, 
they are considered to have been performed. 
- For example, if “gains Power +1000“ is 
infinitely looped, and is chosen to be 
stopped after 200 times, the master of the 
effect does not perform Power +1000 200 
times, but just performs Power +200000. 
18.1.1.5. Great discretion should be exercised in 
recognizing a loop. Both players should agree, 
or a judge’s decision should be sought. 
 
18.2. Extra Turn 
18.2.1. When a player gets an “extra turn“, the extra 
turn for that player is added immediately after 
the current turn. 
18.2.2. If 2 or more turns are added within the same 
turn, the turns will take place from the turn that 
was added from the text that resolved last. 
- For example, if each player resolves the 
text “you get an extra turn“ in the order of 
turn player → non-turn player → turn 
player, the resulting order of turns would 
be “current turn → turn player’s extra turn 
→ non-turn player’s extra turn → turn 
player’s extra turn → non- turn player’s 
turn“. “ 
 
18.3. Number of different cards 
18.3.1. When counting the number of different cards, 
the number of different card names is counted
```

### Page 53

```text
unless a particular type of information to be 
counted is specified. 
18.3.1.1. When counting the number of different 
card names, the number of cards is not 
referenced. 
- For example, if a player is the master of 1 
unit, and it has both the card names 
“Blaster Blade” and “Blaster Arrow”, that 
player has two different “Blaster” card 
names among their units. 
18.3.1.2. If grade or some other information is 
specified, it is determined by that information. 
 
18.4. End Turn Resolution 
18.4.1. If an instruction to end the turn is to be 
performed for any reason during the game, 
perform the following. 
18.4.1.1. End the durations of all continuous effects 
currently active, other than those with the 
durations “until end of turn” or “during this turn” 
or have durations that expire in the next turn or 
later. 
18.4.1.2. End the resolution of the currently 
resolving card or ability. If the ability has 
processes written after this process, they are 
not performed. 
18.4.1.3. If it is not currently the end phase, the 
game moves to the end phase without 
performing a check timing. 
18.4.2. If there is any vanguard damage remaining 
after the end of turn resolution, perform the 
damage application process (13.6) as a rule 
action during the end phase. 
18.4.3. The playing of automatic abilities that are 
standing by (11.9.4) during the end turn 
resolution is performed during the check timing 
of the end phase. 
 
18.5. Putting Set cards as Units on Circles 
18.5.1. It is possible for certain set cards to put as a 
unit on a circle, and it is handled according to the 
following rules. 
18.5.2. When a set card is regarded as a unit, that 
card loses the order main type, loses the special 
types (2.9.5) it had from being an order and set, 
and newly gains the unit main type, and gains 
the subtypes and special types granted by that 
resolution. 
18.5.3. When a set card becomes a unit, it 
possesses the power and critical and shield 
specified by that resolution. 
18.5.3.1. If that resolution did not specify these 
values, the power and critical become 0, and it 
does not have any shield. 
18.5.4. The card put on the circle from this resolution 
is put as the specified unit on the circle. This is a 
new card due to a change in zones, and the 
effects that applied to the set card until now no 
longer apply (4.1.8). 
 
18.6. Rules restricting stride 
18.6.1. Stride may be restricted, such as by the 
Fighter’s Rules, and is handled by the following 
rules. 
18.6.1.1. Even if Stride is restricted for a game, you 
may prepare a G deck for the game, and put 
the G deck in the G zone when preparing for 
the game. 
18.6.1.2. During a game where stride is restricted, 
if there is a rule or effect that moves a card that 
is not in the G zone to the G zone due to the 
end phase or any other reason, that card is 
moved to the G zone according to the normal 
rules (4.4.2). 
18.6.2. Even if stride is restricted by rules, if there is 
a “can perform Stride” state by some effect, you 
can perform stride according to the normal rules 
for stride.
```

```text
as your vanguard become Grade 3/[Power] 
13000/[Critical] 1 units with "Twin Drive", "Persona 
Ride", and all of the following. (They lose all of their 
original [Power] , [Shield] , and abilities) 
・[AUTO](VC):At the beginning of your battle phase, 
reveal the top card of your deck, choose one of your 
opponent's rear-guards with grade less than or equal 
to the revealed card, and until end of your 
opponent's next turn, that unit cannot move to (GC) 
or other (RC), and cannot [Stand] during the stand 
phase. If the revealed card is a normal unit, discard 
it. 
・[CONT](VC):When this unit would attack, it battles 
all of your opponent's front row units.
```

```text
marker is on is retired, you 
search your deck for up to

and shuffle your deck.
```
